 Meanwhile, outside the BHU gate, hundreds of students are protesting
 1200 chaatr-chaatraon par exiaar darj kii gai he
 Apart from various parts of UP, Protests are also happening in Delhi
 is bich, BHU kii ghatana ko lekar pradhanmantri narendra modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah ne uttar pradesh ke mukhyamantri yogi adityanath se baat kii he or jaruri kadam uthaane ko kaha he
 Meanwhile, the Varanasi Police has registered a case against 1200 unidentified students on charges of violent incidents and breach of peace in the BHU campus
 vahiin uniwarsity campus main lathicharge ke liye pehali najar main doshi paae gaye lanka thane ke incharge, bheloopur ke sio or ek atirikt city magistrate ko hataa diya gaya he

 khabar yah bhi he ki chaatr-chaatraon se hostal khaali karaae ja rahe hai or unke bijli-pani kaa conection bhi kaat diya gaya he

 vahiin biechayu ke kulapati ne is puure andolan ko bahari tatwon kii sajeesh bataaya he
 Pro
 girish chandra treepathi ne kaha kii chaatro kaa hangaamaa vishvidhyalay ko badnaam karne kii sajeesh he

 unhone kaha kii updrav kii ghatana bahari logon kii dein he

 unhone kaha ki vishvidhyalay main bahari logon kaa pravesh tab se he, jab se vishvidhyalay bana he

 chaatraon kaa chhedhkhani ke khilaaf pradarshnabata den ki uniwarsity parisar main chaatraon se 'badhati chhedhkhani' kii ghatnaon ke khilaaf yahaan guuruuvaar se hi chaatr-chatraayen virodh pradarshan kar rahi hai

 chaatra ke mutabik, jab usne un logon kaa virodh kiya, to teen logon ne uske saath gaali-galouj kii or uske baad bhaag gaye

 suraksha maangati chaatraon par lathichargein chaatraon kaa aarope he ki unhen campus main lagaataar hi chhedhkhani kaa saamana karnaa padataa he or vishvavidhyalay prashasan asaamaajik tatwon ko rokane ke liye koi karrwai nahin kar rahaa he
 In such a situation, he sat on a 'dharna' near the maingate of the campus at midnight on Thursday, seeking to increase security in the university campus
 in chaatraon ko shant karne kii koshish kaamyaab nahin hone par police ne shanivaar raat chaatraon par lathicharge kar diya

 patrakaron par is kathith lathicharge ke virodh main lakhanu main kuch patrakaron ne mukhyamantri awaas ke saamne dharna diya
